---
title: "FairBid SDK Changelog"
---

Android iOS Unity

## Android Changelog

Get the latest SDK from our [SDK Integration](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/16884209848092-SDK-Integration#h_01JBGYBF89SH95EZTVXKGJEG6T) page.

#### Important

Our Changelogs contain a list of supported network versions from the date of the DT FairBid SDK release. The latest DT FairBid SDK version is always compatible with the most updated supported network versions from our [networks table.](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010077777-Supported-Networks#platform-android)

## Version 3.60.0

24 Apr 2025

***

**Fixed:**

* Occasional crash when checking for ad availability immdiately after FairBid initializaiton.
* Banner ad cropped on Unity6.

**Supported Networks (at time of the DT FairBid SDK release):**

* AdMob/Google Bidding 24.2.0 (updated)
* Amazon Publisher Services 9.10.4
* AppLovin 13.1.0
* BIGO Ads 5.1.0
* Chartboost 9.8.3
* DT Exchange 8.3.7 (updated)
* Google Ad Manager 23.6.0
* HyprMX 6.4.2
* InMobi 10.8.2 (updated)
* IronSource 7.9.0
* Liftoff Monetize 7.4.3 (updated)
* Meta Audience Network 6.18.0
* Mintegral 16.8.61
* MyTarget 5.21.0
* Ogury 6.0.1
* Pangle 6.5.0.5 (updated)
* UnityAds 4.14.0 (updated)
* Verve Group 3.2.1

Please check our [documentation](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010077777-Supported-Networks#platform-ios) for the latest network updates.

## Version 3.59.0

13 Mar 2025

***

**Improvements:**

* Update Ogury GDPR compliance: Leveraging TCFv2 instead of Ogury’s “Choice Manager” (minimum version support bumped to Ogury 6.0.1)

**Fixed:**

* Edge case crash during SDK startup
* Performance improvement around auto-requests

**Supported Networks (at time of the DT FairBid SDK release):**

* AdMob/Google Bidding 23.6.0
* Amazon Publisher Services 9.10.4
* AppLovin 13.1.0 (updated - new minimum version)
* BIGO Ads 5.1.0
* Chartboost 9.8.3 (updated)
* DT Exchange 8.3.6
* Google Ad Manager 23.6.0
* HyprMX 6.4.2
* InMobi 10.8.0 (updated)
* IronSource 7.9.0
* Liftoff Monetize 7.4.2
* Meta Audience Network 6.18.0
* Mintegral 16.8.61
* MyTarget 5.21.0
* Ogury 6.0.1 (updated - new minimum version)
* Pangle 6.4.0.6 (updated)
* UnityAds 4.13.1 (updated)
* Verve Group 3.2.1

Please check our [documentation](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010077777-Supported-Networks#platform-ios) for the latest network updates.

## Version 3.58.2

21 February 2025

***

**Fixed:**

* Missing callbacks when using the BannerView integration and loading the banner before attaching the view to the view hierarchy.



## Version 3.58.1

17 February 2025

***

**Improvements:**

* Enhanced VAST ads experience (supported by [DTExchange version8.3.6](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010834177-DT-Exchange-Android-Changelog#h_01JA8TEQ4CHJ4G4NAJB283PE71)).
* Ad rendering in edge-to-edge mode on Android 15 devices (supported by [DTExchange version8.3.6](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010834177-DT-Exchange-Android-Changelog#h_01JA8TEQ4CHJ4G4NAJB283PE71)).

**Fixed:**

* Crash when requesting an ad immediately after SDK starts.



## Version 3.58.0

28 January 2025

***

**Improvements:**

* Added ability to reuse instance names and IDs for bidding networks (supported by v 3.56.0+).

**Fixed:**

* FairBid and DT-X not adhering to Google Ads Policy guidelines on limited ad tracking
* All callbacks are now guaranteed to be dispatched on the main thread

**Supported Networks (at time of the DT FairBid SDK release):**

* AdMob/Google Bidding 23.6.0 (updated)
* Amazon Publisher Services 9.10.4 (updated)
* AppLovin 13.0.1
* BIGO Ads 5.1.0 (updated)
* Chartboost 9.8.2 (updated)
* DT Exchange 8.3.5 (updated)
* Google Ad Manager 23.6.0
* HyprMX 6.4.2 (updated)
* InMobi 10.7.5 (updated)
* IronSource 7.9.0
* Liftoff Monetize 7.4.2
* Meta Audience Network 6.18.0
* Mintegral 16.8.61
* MyTarget 5.21.0
* Ogury 5.8.0
* Pangle 6.4.0.5 (updated)
* UnityAds 4.12.5 (updated)
* Verve Group 3.2.1 (updated)



## Version 3.57.1

8 January 2025

***

**Fixed:**

* Possible crash related to **play-services-ads-identifier** (version18.2.0) on devices running Android7 and earlier.
* Various stability fixes and improvements from [DTExchange8.3.4](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010834177-DT-Exchange-Android-Changelog#h_01JA8TEQ4CHJ4G4NAJB283PE71).

## Version 3.57.0

13 December 2024

***

**Improvements:**

* FairBid now supports AppLovin SDK 13.0.1, and if user is a child, FairBid does not start the ApplovinSDK.

#### Note

To consider a user as a child, the FairBid SDK relies on both the `.setUserAChild()` and `.disableAdvertisingId()` APIs when initializing the FairBid SDK. For more information about these APIs, see [Advanced Initialization Options](/hc/en-us/articles/16847944034204).

* Added support for GAM resellers.
* Test Suite provides more reliable test mode and feedback for AppLovin.

**Supported Networks (at time of the DT FairBid SDK release):**

* AdMob/Google Bidding 23.5.0 (updated)
* Amazon Publisher Services 9.9.2
* AppLovin 13.0.1 (updated)
* BIGO Ads 4.8.0
* Chartboost 9.7.0
* [DT Exchange 8.3.3](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010834177-DT-Exchange-Android-Changelog#h_01JA8TEQ4CHJ4G4NAJB283PE71)
* Google Ad Manager 23.5.0 (updated)
* HyprMX 6.4.1
* InMobi 10.6.3
* IronSource 7.9.0
* Liftoff Monetize 7.4.2 (updated)
* Meta Audience Network 6.18.0
* Mintegral 16.8.61 (updated)
* MyTarget 5.21.0
* Ogury 5.8.0
* Pangle 6.1.0.9
* UnityAds 4.12.3
* Verve Group 2.21.1

Please check our [documentation](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010077777-Supported-Networks#platform-android) for the latest network updates.

## Version 3.46.0

***

**Improvements:**

* Support for interstitials, rewarded ads and banners from BIGO Ads
* Removed support for Tapjoy
* Several performance and stability improvements
* Upgraded DT Exchange renderer to version 8.2.5
  * Updated OMSDK to v1.4.9

**Fixed:**

* Fixes a banner refresh issue with banner ads from IronSource where requests would result in a timeout
* Improved handling of WebView crashes

## Version 3.44.1

25 October 2023

***

**Improvements:**

* Improved performance and error handling when showing ads that became unavailable
* Support for InMobi’s US Privacy String API
* The request callback now contains a request ID parameter, which is the same as the impression data in the show callback

**Fixed:**

* Incompatibility with Android Gradle Plugin 8.0.0+
* Fixes issues when InMobi and Liftoff are showing ads and a new ad request is already running
* Memory leaks in banner refresh and the Test Suite
* Malicious error handling a rare issue when displaying full-screen ads that do not respond
* Rare crash on banners

**Supported Networks (at the time of the DT FairBid SDK release):**

* AdColony 4.8.0
* AdMob/Google Bidding 22.4.0 (updated)
* Amazon Publisher Services 9.8.3
* AppLovin 11.10.1
* Chartboost 9.3.1
* DT Exchange 8.2.4
* Google Ad Manager 22.4.0
* HyprMX 6.2.0
* InMobi 10.5.8
* IronSource 7.5.1
* Liftoff Monetize 6.12.1
* Meta Audience Network 6.16.0
* Mintegral 16.5.21 (updated)
* MyTarget 5.18.0
* Ogury 5.6.0
* Pangle 5.4.1.1 (updated)
* Tapjoy 13.1.2
* UnityAds 4.9.1 (updated)
* Verve Group 2.18.1

Please check our [documentation](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010077777-Supported-Networks#platform-android) for the latest network updates.

## Version 3.41.2

02 August 2023

***

## Version 3.25.0

15 March 2022

***

**Improvements**:

* Added support for banner placement type for Mintegral bidder. This is in addition to the existing support for interstitial and rewarded placement types
* Added support for Mintegral’s "New Interstitial" ad format
* Improved handling of delayed network SDK starts
* Performance improvements
* Upgraded Fyber Marketplace renderer to version 8.1.3
* Removed old media cache which had an open localhost socket listening on a random high port. As such, having a localhost exception role in the network security config is no longer required.
* Various stability fixes and improvements

**Fixed**:

* Rare crash on some Huawei devices
* Possible ANR crash related to OM SDK initialization
* Crash related to a 3rd party SDK that overrides our network stack and causes a failure when parsing ad response

19 January 2022

***

#### Integration

From version 3.23.1, the Android integration is changing. You must integrate a plugin instead of an SDK.

This plugin can be integrated by adding the following code to your application gradle build script (for more details, click [here](https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/plugins.html#sec:plugins_block)).

Using the plugins DSL:

```python
plugins {
  id 'com.fyber.fairbid-sdk-plugin' version '3.23.1'
}

repositories {
  mavenCentral()
}
```

  * Upgraded Fyber Marketplace renderer to version 8.1.2

**Fixed:**

* * * Various crashes related to OMSDK
    * Various stability fixes and improvements

## Version 3.16.0

21 June 2021

***

**Improvements**:

* * * [Pangle](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360020569718-Pangle) is a new supported Network for Banner, Interstitial and Rewarded mediation
    * FairBid sets Verizon’s "collectionMode" for GDPR opt-in, thus abolishing the need to handle that separately in the app
    * Follow IAB standard when storing CCPA string in the app and sharing it with mediation partners
    * Upgraded Fyber Marketplace renderer to version 7.8.3
    * Rewarded Videos longer than 30 seconds will now be accepted on Fyber Marketplace and a skip button will be displayed at the 30-second mark
    * Removed VPAID support

**Fixed**:

* * * Crash when network is configured on the dashboard but SDK not integrated
    * Global auto-request setting when disabled is overridden when bringing application to the foreground
    * First banner auto retry is triggered after wrong interval upon erron on show
    * Banner onError is not called under certain conditions on first request
    * Issue synchonizing Placement requests and initialization of adapters
    * Marketplace Fixes
    * Rare internal SDK race condition that caused no impression callback to be invoked in VAST creatives
    * Possible ANR related to GMS QueryInfo
    * Bug that caused some image end cards in full screen ads to not display
    * MRAID open errors will now include a proper error message
    * spot.isReady() will now properly return true when a SCAR API Banner is ready to render
    * Stability and Crash issues

## Version 3.14.0

13 April 2021

***

**Improvements**:

* Waterfall optimization: Caching instances’ “no fill/response'' of a given waterfall to optimize the next waterfall and by so reducing latency and improving the performance of waterfalls with multiple instances
* Applying auto-request for interstitial and rewarded video ad formats at the moment an ad is being shown to reduce latency between sequential ads display
* Deprecate 'clearGDPRConsent' API, use 'setGdprConsentString' API instead

**Fixed**:

* Workaround for issues with AdMob’s “mute” API (sets ad volume to zero)

## Version 3.13.0

17 March 2021

***

From FairBid SDK version 3.13.0, the FairBid SDK will automatically retry to load the first banners for you. When a banner is requested and you don't get a fill, Fyber adopts a backoff mechanism and retries until we get a fill or you explicitly call the ‘destroy’ method. After the first banner is successfully shown, it continues refreshing as usual.

**Improvements**:

* * * * * Banners: retry logic on first request (see details above).
        * Support for [InMobi](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010078017#inmobi-0-9) as a mediated bidding network. Supporting banner, interstitial, and rewarded ad formats
        * Google AdMob: [Adaptive Banners](https://developers.google.com/admob/ios/banner/adaptive) support.

**Fixed**:

* * * * * In cases where the value of GDPR consent is unknown, the type of ads for Chartboost, InMobi and Fyber Marketplace are restricted.
        * Rare side-effects when enabling/disabling [auto-request](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360009940017-Auto-Request) for one placement on other placements auto-request behaviour.

**Android Supported Networks**:

* * * * * AdColony 4.4.1
        * AdMob 19.7.0
        * AppLovin 9.15.3
        * Chartboost 8.2.0
        * Facebook Audience Network 6.3.0
        * InMobi 9.1.6
        * IronSource 7.1.1
        * Mintegral 15.4.51
        * MyTarget 5.11.12
        * Ogury 5.0.6
        * Snap 1.0.3.5
        * Tapjoy 12.7.1
        * UnityAds 3.6.0
        * Verizon 1.9.0
        * Vungle 6.8.1

**Improvements**:

        * New:
        * Enhanced video skipability enforcement mechanism
        * Enhanced user experience with larger video button controls on tablets
        * (7.8.0):
        * Added additional Contextual parameters and improved the infrastructure
        * Redesigned our network stack implementation with significant improvements. Impacts all network communications (i.e ad requests, tracking events, and more)
        * Ignore unsupported spots ad requests (i.e. support videos only for Interstitial and Rewarded)
        * Increased Target APIs to Android 10, to meet Google Play’s Target API Level Requirements
        * Fixed:
        * Improved handling of deeplink URLs
        * Crash related to memory allocation
        * Various bug fixes
        * 7.8.0
        * Various crashes related to MRAID and VPAID
        * Issue where video player icons were cropped on some devices
        * Miscellaneous improvements and stability fixes
        * 7.7.4
        * Fixed a crash in banners when calling bindView for a webview which crashed

**Fixed**:

        * Crash related to the banner life cycle in apps using Flutter framework

## Version 3.11.0

18 January 2021

***

**Improvements**:

* * * * * Preventing Unity Ads 3.5 and above to run on APIs lower than 19. For more information, click [here](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010172138-Unity-Ads)
        * Extended Impression Level Data API to expose the “variant Id”. For more information, click [here](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010150517-Impression-Level-Data).
        * Exposed Impression Level Data API through a new API that can be called before the impression takes place. For more information, click [here](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010150517-Impression-Level-Data).
        * Added new API for passing custom key/value parameters when showing Interstitials and Rewarded ads. For more information, click [here](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360017107958).

**Fixed**:

* * * * * Build error when integrating both FairBid and Ofw Edge SDKs
        * Crash when changing auto-request behaviour through the public API concurrently with SDK logic triggered by application lifecycle events.
        * Misleading error logs when trying to show an ad that has not been yet requested

## Version 3.0

31 March 2020

***

**Updates**:

* * * * * Source and target compatibility must be set for Java 1.8 in integrations supporting Android SDK lower than 26. More information in our integration page

**Improvements**:

* * * * * Improved ad delivery and fill management performance
        * Requesting programmatic AdColony instances from the test suite
        * Test Suite better helps to check for successful integration on Android 9+
        * Upgraded Fyber Marketplace renderer to version 7.5.3:
        * Deep Links of type "intent" with a fallback URL will open the fallback URL, if the target application is not installed on the device
        * Support added for CompanionClickTracking
        * Fullscreen activity now requires hardware acceleration. No developer action required
        * Improved deep link handling
        * VPAID is now supported in the mute API
        * Using ExoPlayer for rendering VAST ads

**Fixed**:

* * * * * FAN ad objects were not properly destroyed
        * Fyber banner impression not sent when app context was lost
        * Destroyed banners interfered with other banners
        * Programmatic instances in test suite timed out
        * Fixes banner user experience issue when same banner was requested twice
        * Minor issues in the waterfall process
        * Click logic has been revised
        * Fixed a crash related to the cancelling of ad requests in very particular timings.
        * Fixed a potential crash in the video cache mechanism
        * Potential crash when calling webview getSettings API

**Android Supported Network Updates**:

* * * * * AdMob 19.0.0
        * Chartboost 8.0.1
        * Facebook 5.7.1
        * ironSource 6.15.0.1
        * Mintegral 13.0.01
        * Vungle 6.5.2

## Version: 2.6.0

20 January 2020

***

**Updates**

        * When hosting activity has a launch mode of “singleTask” ads displayed will now properly dismiss when required.
        * Removal of the GSON dependency
        * Using ExoPlayer for rendering VAST ads

**Fixed**

* * * * * onHide callback fired before onCompletion for Fyber demand
        * Adapters not starting correctly when initialization was interrupted by a foreign activity
        * Click logic has been revised
        * Fixed a crash related to the cancelling of ad requests in very particular timings.
        * Fixed a potential crash in the video cache mechanism.
        * Improved rendering of full screen html ads
        * Better handling of Google Play click URLs inside the ad
        * Interstitial ads cannot be dismissed before given an opportunity to be visible to the user
        * Full screen interstitials display ads are not scrollable
        * Intent scheme is properly sent to the operating system
        * Fixed a possible ANR on devices running Android 5.x
        * Renamed a package which was possibly conflicting with other open source package names.
        * Stability improvements

## Version 3.57.0

13 December 2024

***

**Improvements:**

* FairBid no longer supports iOS 11.
* If the user is a child, FairBid does not start the ApplovinSDK.

#### Note

To consider a user as a child, the FairBid SDK relies on both the `.setUserAChild()` and `.disableAdvertisingId()` APIs when initializing the FairBid SDK. For more information about these APIs, see [Advanced Initialization Options](/hc/en-us/articles/16847944034204).

* Added support for GAM resellers.

* Test Suite provides improved search features to recognize substrings in Placement types.

* Added support for [DTExchange8.3.4](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010922578-DT-Exchange-iOS-Changelog):

  * Added **Auto StoreKit** feature for full-screen Display Ads.
  * Added **SKOverlay** support for full-screen Display Ads.

**Fixed:**

* Ogury reporting now correctly distinguishes between `show` errors and `load` errors.

**Supported Networks (at time of the DT FairBid SDK release):**

* AdMob/Google Bidding 11.10.0
* Amazon Publisher Services 4.9.0
* AppLovin 13.0.0

## Version 3.44.1

25 October 2023

***

#### Note

We have ensured that this version is fully compatible with iOS 17. (Technically, previous versions are also compatible with iOS 17.)

**Improvements:**

* Improved performance and error handling when showing ads that became unavailable
* Support for InMobi’s US Privacy String API
* The request callback now contains a request ID parameter, which is the same as in the impression data in the show callback.
* ‘bannerDidLoad’ callback now contains ‘impressionData’

**Fixed:**

* Prevent potential banner memory leaks related to ‘presentingViewController’
* Rare crash after a previous crash that happened under a different SDK version

## Version 3.16.0

21 June 2021

***

**Improvements**:

* * * * * [Pangle](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360020569718-Pangle) is a new supported Network for Banner, Interstitial and Rewarded mediation
        * FairBid sets Verizon’s "collectionMode" for GDPR opt-in, thus abolishing the need to handle that separately in the app
        * Follow IAB standard when storing CCPA string in the app and sharing it with mediation partners
        * Upgraded Fyber Marketplace renderer to version 7.8.6

**Fixed**:

* * * * * InMobi Banner ad being dismissed upon click
        * Waterfall instance no-fill caching uses wrong interval
        * Test Suite does not show correct auction result in “Placements” view when a mediated network wins
        * Test Suite request statuses are not shown when "Request/Show" button is hit during the ongoing waterfall audit
        * Marketplace Fixes
        * Crash in SKAdNetwork version 2.2 when the application is running on iOS 14.5.0 and the store product is in an unsupported region
        * Crash occurring in cases where the application uses an AdMob version below 7.64.0 with Fyber Marketplace SDK version 7.8.3.

## Version 3.15.0

26 May 2021

***

**Improvements**:

* * * * * New in Test Suite - "Placements" section to test the Placement Instance set-up of your app. Run a real-time FairBid auction on an ad request to your test device and verify that the Instances are set and called as expected. For more details, click [here](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360009940677-Test-Suite).

**Fixed**:

* * * * * InMobi adapter does not load bidder markup
        * Banners in Test Suite are not shown correctly on some devices
        * Other Placement’s availability is not updated when current ad is shown, but only when it is closed
        * "Unavailable" callback is not fired in some rare cases
        * Impression data API returns "nil" when used from within "isAvailable" callback

## Version 3.14.0

13 April 2021

***

For Apps that have set Auto-Request enabled Placements with AppLovin Instances, we recommend not integrate 3.14.0, as an issue was discovered. SDK version 3.14.1 includes a fix and is scheduled to be released during the week of 3 - 7 May.

**Improvements**:

* * * * * Waterfall optimization: Caching instances’ “no fill/response'' of a given waterfall to optimize the next waterfall and by so reducing latency and improving the performance of waterfalls with multiple instances
        * Applying auto-request for interstitial and rewarded video ad formats at the moment an ad is being shown to reduce latency between sequential ads display
        * Deprecated 'clearGDPRConsent' API, use GDPRConsentString' API instead
        * More detailed Verizon SDK version info reported in the test suite

**Fixed**:

* * * * * Workaround for issues with AdMob’s “mute” API (sets ad volume to zero)
        * AdMob test mode not working when IDFA is not available
        * Verizon: wrong handling of modal view callbacks
        * Verizon: UI API called from background thread
        * Missing InMobi error on show callback
        * Missing IronSource error on show callback
        * Missing Verizon error on show callback
        * Missing Mintegral error on show callback
        * Clicks not reported for Tapjoy ads

**iOS Supported Networks**: (At the time of the FairBid SDK release)

## Version 3.13.0

17 March 2021

***

From FairBid SDK version 3.13.0, the FairBid SDK will automatically retry to load the first banners for you. When a banner is requested and you don't get a fill, Fyber adopts a backoff mechanism and retries until we get a fill or you explicitly call the ‘destroy’ method. After the first banner is successfully shown, it continues refreshing as usual.

**Improvements**:

* * * * * Banners: retry logic on first request (see details above).
        * Support for [InMobi](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010078017#inmobi-0-9) as a mediated bidding network. Supporting banner, interstitial, and rewarded ad formats
        * Google AdMob: [Adaptive Banners](https://developers.google.com/admob/ios/banner/adaptive) support.
        * Reduced waterfall latency by caching ads from mediated networks.

**Fixed**:

* * * * * In cases where the value of GDPR consent is unknown, the type of ads for AdColony, InMobi and Fyber Marketplace are restricted.

**iOS Supported Networks**:

* * * * * AdColony 4.5.0
        * AdMob 8.1.0
        * AppLovin 6.15.2
        * Chartboost 8.4.1
        * Facebook Audience Network 6.3.0
        * InMobi 9.1.5
        * IronSource 7.1.1.0
        * Mintegral 6.7.6.0
        * MyTarget 5.9.11
        * Ogury 2.3.3
        * Snap 1.0.7
        * Tapjoy 12.7.1
        * UnityAds 3.6.0
        * Verizon 1.9.0
        * Vungle 6.9.1

## Version 3.57.0

13 December 2024

***

**Improvements:**

* AppLoving SDK Support:

  * (Android) FairBid now supports AppLovin SDK 13.0.1, and if user is a child, FairBid does not start the ApplovinSDK.
  * (iOS) If the user is a child, FairBid does not start the ApplovinSDK.

  #### Note

  To consider a user as a child, the FairBid SDK relies on both the `.setUserAChild()` and `.disableAdvertisingId()` APIs when initializing the FairBid SDK. For more information about these APIs, see [Advanced Initialization Options](/hc/en-us/articles/16847944034204).

* (Android and iOS) Added support for GAM resellers.

* (iOS) FairBid no longer supports iOS 11.

* Test Suite improvements:

* * (Android) Test Suite provides more reliable test mode and feedback for AppLovin.
  * (iOS) Test Suite provides improved search features to recognize substrings in Placement types.

  (iOS) Added support for [DT Exchange 8.3.4](https://developer.digitalturbine.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010922578-DT-Exchange-iOS-Changelog):

  * Added **Auto StoreKit** feature for full-screen Display Ads.
  * Added **SKOverlay** support for full-screen Display Ads.

**Fixed:**

* (iOS) Ogury reporting now correctly distinguishes between `show` errors and `load` errors.

**Supported Android Networks (at time of the DT FairBid SDK release):**

* AdMob/Google Bidding 23.5.0 (updated)

    * (Android and iOS) Impressionid inside Impression Data should never be null
    * (iOS) Show missing SKAdNetowrk IDs in Test Suite
    * (Android) Upgraded Fyber Marketplace renderer to version 8.1.5
    * Support of VAST wrappers ClickThrough in case it is missing in the in-line VAST

**Fixed**:

* * * (Android) Crash on Amazon devices when using AdMob 20.6.0
    * (Android) UnityAds Rewarded Video fails to show
    * (iOS) FairBid SDK does not retry config request on init under some circumstances
    * (iOS) .xcframework does not contain library definitions for ios-arm64-simulator
    * (iOS) Test suite placement screen crash

    * (Android) Crash related to a 3rd party SDK that overrides our network stack and causes a failure when parsing ad response

* * * Android 3.24.0
    * iOS 3.24.0

**Improvements**:

* * * (Unity) Separated the native SDKs from the Unity Plugin

      This enables the xcframework format on iOS allowing support for simulators on M1 architecture.

      The Unity Plugin is now more lightweight and resilient. However, as of this version, you must add an extra step to ensure the native SDKs are integrated successfully.

    * (Android and iOS) Added support for Mintegral Banners (Bidding coming soon)

    * (iOS) Upgraded Fyber Marketplace renderer to version 8.1.3

    * Added support for (Open Measurement) OMSDK v1.3.26

    * (iOS) Crash in FMPLogger when SKAdNetwork's 'startImpression' failed

## Version 3.23.1

19 January 2022

***

The FairBid SDK plugin must be added to your project.

You must declare the following plugin in your mainTemplate.gradle file, in exactly the same way that you would for a native integration:

```python
plugins {
   ...
   id 'com.fyber.fairbid-sdk-plugin' version '3.23.1'
   ...
}
```

**Improvements**:

* * * (Android and iOS) Support of Pangle bidder for Banners, Interstitials and Rewarded Ads

    * (Android) Support for OMSDK v1.3.28

**Fixes**:

* * * (Android) Various crashes related to OMSDK
    * (Android) Various stability fixes and improvements
    * (iOS) Rare crash in the waterfall logic
    * (iOS) Applovin fullscreen ads freeze the app on click

## Version 3.16.0

21 June 2021

***

**Improvements**:

* * * (Android and iOS) [Pangle](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360020569718-Pangle) is a new supported Network for Banner, Interstitial and Rewarded mediation
    * (Android and iOS) FairBid sets Verizon’s "collectionMode" for GDPR opt-in, thus abolishing the need to handle that separately in the app
    * (Android and iOS) Follow IAB standard when storing CCPA string in the app and sharing it with mediation partners
    * (Android) Upgraded Fyber Marketplace renderer to version 7.8.3
    * Rewarded Videos longer than 30 seconds will now be accepted on Fyber Marketplace and a skip button will be displayed at the 30-second mark
    * Removed VPAID support
    * (iOS)Upgraded Fyber Marketplace renderer to version 7.8.6

**Fixed**:

* * * (Android) Crash when network is configured on the dashboard but SDK not integrated
    * (Android) Global auto-request setting when disabled is overridden when bringing application to the foreground
    * (Android) First banner auto retry is triggered after wrong interval upon erron on show
    * (Android) Banner onError is not called under certain conditions on first request
    * (Android) Issue synchonizing Placement requests and initialization of adapters
    * (Android) Marketplace Fixes
    * Rare internal SDK race condition that caused no impression callback to be invoked in VAST creatives
    * Possible ANR related to GMS QueryInfo
    * Bug that caused some image end cards in full screen ads to not display
    * MRAID open errors will now include a proper error message
    * spot.isReady() will now properly return true when a SCAR API Banner is ready to render
    * Stability and Crash issues
    * (iOS) InMobi Banner ad being dismissed upon click
    * (iOS) Waterfall instance no-fill caching uses wrong interval
    * (iOS) Test Suite does not show correct auction result in “Placements” view when a mediated network wins
    * (iOS) Test Suite request statuses are not shown when "Request/Show" button is hit during the ongoing waterfall audit
    * (iOS) Marketplace Fixes
    * Crash in SKAdNetwork version 2.2 when the application is running on iOS 14.5.0 and the store product is in an unsupported region
    * Crash occurring in cases where the application uses an AdMob version below 7.64.0 with Fyber Marketplace SDK version 7.8.3.

## Version 3.13.0

17 March 2021

***

From FairBid SDK version 3.13.0, the FairBid SDK will automatically retry to load the first banners for you. When a banner is requested and you don't get a fill, Fyber adopts a backoff mechanism and retries until we get a fill or you explicitly call the ‘destroy’ method. After the first banner is successfully shown, it continues refreshing as usual.

**Improvements**:

* * * (Android and iOS) Banners: retry logic on first request (see details above).
    * (Android and iOS) Support for [InMobi](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360010078017#inmobi-0-9) as a mediated bidding network. Supporting banner, interstitial, and rewarded ad formats
    * (Android and iOS) Google AdMob: [Adaptive Banners](https://developers.google.com/admob/ios/banner/adaptive) support.
    * (iOS)Reduced waterfall latency by caching ads from mediated networks.

**Fixed**:

* * * (Android and iOS) In cases where the value of GDPR consent is unknown, the type of ads for Chartboost, InMobi and Fyber Marketplace are restricted.
    * (Android and iOS) Rare side-effects when enabling/disabling [auto-request](https://developer.fyber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360009940017-Auto-Request) for one placement on other placements auto-request behaviour.

**Android Supported Networks**:

* * * AdColony 4.4.1
    * AdMob 19.7.0
    * AppLovin 9.15.3
    * Chartboost 8.2.0
    * Facebook Audience Network 6.3.0
    * InMobi 9.1.6
    * IronSource 7.1.1
    * Mintegral 15.4.51
    * MyTarget 5.11.12
    * Ogury 5.0.6
    * Snap 1.0.3.5
    * Tapjoy 12.7.1
    * UnityAds 3.6.0
    * Verizon 1.9.0
    * Vungle 6.8.1

**iOS Supported Networks**:

* * * AdColony 4.5.0
    * AdMob 8.1.0
    * AppLovin 6.15.2
    * Chartboost 8.4.1
    * Facebook Audience Network 6.3.0
    * InMobi 9.1.5

***

**Improvements**:

      * Added support for dark mode in in-app browser
      * User interface updates targeting increased user engagement (Video CTA now lists “Install Now” instead of “Visit Us” )
      * Added improved user experience for video by adding swipe to open StoreKit and StoreKit video end cards
      * Improved click handling for interstitial display Ad Units
      * Improved the SDK handling of VAST CompanionAd file extension and mime-types, such as case-insensitive “JPG”
      * Improved the look and feel of the fail-safe close button

**Fixed**:

* * * AdMob Banner not rendered in Test Suite
    * Fixed a crash in the Verizon adapter that occurred in some Interstitial scenarios
    * Fixed a crash when showing a Placement without a fill while an ad is being displayed
    * Fixes to the Fyber Marketplace renderer
    * * Fixed a crash in a certain rare scenario while opening the StoreKit
      * Fixed a crash in a certain rare scenario when showing the in-app browser
      * Fixed a bug with a disappearing close button in the CompanionAd
      * Fixed a bug with missing close button when rotating the device in a certain rare scenario
      * Improved handling of universal link stability. In rare cases users would see a stuck spinner
      * Removed false-positive "page is not available" label from the in-app browser
      * Critical bug that caused the SDK to consider secure app-store links as non-secure.
      * Bug related to missing bundle resources (buttons) in the Unity 2019 integration
      * Increased the close button size and touch area in static end-cards
      UnityAds adapter not working, when configured only for Banners

## Version 3.0

31 March 2020

***

**Improvements**:

* * * * * * * * * Improved ad delivery and fill management performance
                * Requesting programmatic AdColony instances from the test suite
                * Test Suite better helps to check for successful integration on Android 9+
                * Upgraded Fyber Marketplace renderer to version Android 7.5.3
                * Deep Links of type "intent" with a fallback URL will open the fallback URL, if the target application is not installed on the device
                * Support added for CompanionClickTracking
                * Fullscreen activity now requires hardware acceleration. No developer action required
                * Improved deep link handling
                * VPAID is now supported in the mute API
                * Using ExoPlayer for rendering VAST ads
                * Upgraded Fyber Marketplace renderer to version iOS 7.5.4
                * Improved UI/UX for the location of the “close” button in iPhone X and above
                * Improved full-screen video countdown timer logic
                * Improved visual display on banners by adding support for content aware backgrounds
                * Improved memory management in VPAID ads
                * Support added for CompanionClickTracking
                * Ad experience UI update: All 'X' (close) buttons on full screen ads use the same theme
                * When the user closes the landing page / app store of a full screen display ad the SDK dismisses the ad

**Fixed**:

* * * * * * * * * FAN ad objects were not properly destroyed
                * Fyber banner impression not sent when app context was lost
                * Destroyed banners interfered with other banners
                * Programmatic instances in test suite timed out
                * Fixes banner user experience issue when same banner was requested twice
                * Minor issues in the waterfall process
                * Click logic has been revised
                * Fixed a crash related to the cancelling of ad requests in very particular timings.
                * Fixed a potential crash in the video cache mechanism
                * Potential crash when calling webview getSettings API
                * Crash on banner refresh when superview was lost
                * AppLovin 6.9.5 crash in test suite
                * Crash in click-handling module which could occur in certain rare scenarios
                * Bug when using the Smartlink feature, the SDK opens the internal browser instead of the external browser
                * Bug in VPAID with the ‘X’ button which is shown immediately on the endcard (appears after 3 seconds)
                * Bug in iOS 11 when clicking the ‘Visit us’ button only the 1st click responds
                * A potential UI flow on a background thread in certain cases in video flow
                * Bug - audio continues to play when display (MRAID and Video) ad is closed

## Version: 2.6.0

20 January 2020

***

**Updates**

* * * * * * * * * [CCPA](https://dev-unity.fyber.com/docs/ccpa-consent-settings)compliant IAB US privacy string API
                * When hosting activity has a launch mode of “singleTask” ads displayed will now properly dismiss when required.
                * Removal of the GSON dependency
                * Using ExoPlayer for rendering VAST ads
                * Added support for MRAID force orientation
                * Restored the StoreKit usage in iOS 13 and above
                * Added support for dynamic web styling for AB-testing, to test and improve HTML rendering
                * The minimum supported iOS version is now iOS 9
                * Improved overall stability
                * Improved the creatives rendering

**Fixed**

* * * * * * * * * onHide callback fired before onCompletion for Fyber demand
                * Adapters not starting correctly when initialization was interrupted by a foreign activity
                * Tapjoy ad request timeout rate
                * Click logic has been revised
                * Fixed a crash related to the cancelling of ad requests in very particular timings.
                * Fixed a potential crash in the video cache mechanism.
                * Improved rendering of full screen html ads
                * Better handling of Google Play click URLs inside the ad
                * Interstitial ads cannot be dismissed before given an opportunity to be visible to the user
                * Full screen interstitials display ads are not scrollable
                * Intent scheme is properly sent to the operating system
                * Fixed a possible ANR on devices running Android 5.x
                * Renamed a package which was possibly conflicting with other open source package names.
                * Stability improvements
                * Fixed a bug in VPAID which blocked VPAID ads from being rendered on iPads
                * Fixed a bug where the in-app browser was opened upon the 204 response upon the ad click
                * Fixed a minor MRAID sizing bug
                * Stability and performance improvements
                * Fixed inconsistency with User Agents
                * Fixed a crash which could occur in a certain edge case
                * Improved internal browser behavior
                * Improved HTML rendering in certain cases
                * Crash, caused by a specific type of URI for an external app
                * Deprecated: Removed the Automatic Location Update Engine, which required the sensitive location permissions to be added to the info.plist of the publisher application.

***

**Updates**

                * Click[here](https://fyber-mediation.fyber.com/docs/child-related-regulations-1)for additional information about providing child-related settings for AdMob and Facebook.

**Fixed**

* * * * * * * * * UnityAds timeouts on no fills
                * UnityAds clicks not reported for Interstitial and Rewarded
                * FairBid SDK 2.4.0 not compatible with Fyber Offer Wall

                * Mintegral Interstitial ad closed callback not fired
                * Mintegral ads too early reported as ready (Interstitial, Rewarded)
                * Programmatic mediation support for Mintegral
